< Review>
This place is a hit and miss. Depending on the day you go there, you may be fed like a human, other days you go it's sure to be a long wait and the people are rude. It's almost as if the person making the schedule put all the pleasant volunteers on certain days and all the unpleasant ones on the other remaining days.

Example: they ask if you have a place to refrigerate food, and even if you say no , they'll still give you perishables. So, for someone homeless, which is the majority of their clients, you have to either eat it all then or let it sour.

That's not helping the community. There are other places in the area that have realized this error and made efforts or changes to their program. Not this place though.

Without Betty, this place is not what it once was.<//Review>

<user_id>104375966059195277136</user_id><username>Leticia Ley</username><date>1580845775317</date><Rating>5</Rating>< Review>
Love that Lady M Cake Boutique is conveniently located inside Santa Anita Mall.

We decided to pick up a few cakes from here to celebrate Lunar New Year and my dad's birthday. We chose the matcha and the seasonal red bean mille crepe cakes.

The presentation at Lady M is simple, clean and elegant. We love the simplicity of their cakes and the depth of the flavors. You can buy whole cakes and slices. If you are going to buy whole cakes, make sure you go earlier during the day as they run out fast.

My all-time favorite mille crepe cake is the matcha. It's full of matcha flavor, slightly sweet that complements the matcha flavor. The top of the cake is dusted with more matcha powder. If you are a big matcha lover like me, this is the cake you will want to get.

The seasonal red bean mille crepe cake had the cream from their original mille crepe cake along with red bean paste and red bean.

Keep in mind that the prices of cakes tend to be on the high side, Lady M Cake Boutique is definitely a splurge.<//Review>

< Text>
Been going there since I was a boy, the employee's know me and my family by sight. Always friendly and helpful, got my first pair of Smith and Wesson cuffs there.
Their military surplus selection has yielded some rare gems to my collection,  for people who do things like wasteland weekend this place is a must see.

I always joked with the workers that there is always the biggest rush in the store after an earthquake or similar.

This place is where I did a lot of my "zombie apocalypse" prepping. The current pandemic is anti-climatic at the moment. Still thanks to places like this when it started I didn't really need to leave my apartment for a month unless I wanted to or had some where I really needed to be in person.<//Text>
